module: srl_nokia-acl
  +--rw acl
     +--rw acl-filter* [name type]
     |  +--rw name                     string
     |  +--rw type                     enumeration
     |  +--rw description?             srl_nokia-comm:description
     |  +--rw subinterface-specific?   enumeration {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     |  +--rw statistics-per-entry?    boolean {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     |  +--ro last-clear?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  +--rw entry* [sequence-id]
     |     +--rw sequence-id     uint32
     |     +--rw description?    srl_nokia-comm:description
     |     +--ro last-clear?     srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |     +--rw match
     |     |  +--rw l2 {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     |     |  |  +--rw destination-mac
     |     |  |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:mac-address
     |     |  |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:mac-address
     |     |  |  +--rw ethertype?         srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ethertype
     |     |  |  +--rw source-mac
     |     |  |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:mac-address
     |     |  |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:mac-address
     |     |  |  +--rw vlan
     |     |  |     +--rw outermost-vlan-id
     |     |  |        +--rw (vlan-matching-type)?
     |     |  |           +--:(range-with-one-value)
     |     |  |           |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |           |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:vlan-id-type
     |     |  |           +--:(range-with-two-values)
     |     |  |           |  +--rw range
     |     |  |           |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:vlan-id-type
     |     |  |           |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:vlan-id-type
     |     |  |           +--:(special-value-none-to-match-untagged)
     |     |  |              +--rw none?       empty
     |     |  +--rw ipv4
     |     |  |  +--rw destination-ip
     |     |  |  |  +--rw prefix?        srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |     |  |  |  +--rw prefix-list* [name] {srl_nokia-feat:acl-ip-prefix-list}?
     |     |  |  |  |  +--rw name    -> /acl/match-list/ipv4-prefix-list/name
     |     |  |  |  +--rw address?       srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  |  |  +--rw mask?          srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  |  +--rw dscp-set*         srl_nokia-comm:dscp {srl_nokia-feat:ip-acl-dscp-set}?
     |     |  |  +--rw fragment?         boolean
     |     |  |  +--rw first-fragment?   boolean
     |     |  |  +--rw icmp
     |     |  |  |  +--rw type?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:icmp-type
     |     |  |  |  +--rw code*   uint8
     |     |  |  +--rw protocol?         srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ip-protocol-type
     |     |  |  +--rw source-ip
     |     |  |     +--rw prefix?        srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |     |  |     +--rw prefix-list* [name] {srl_nokia-feat:acl-ip-prefix-list}?
     |     |  |     |  +--rw name    -> /acl/match-list/ipv4-prefix-list/name
     |     |  |     +--rw address?       srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  |     +--rw mask?          srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  +--rw ipv6
     |     |  |  +--rw destination-ip
     |     |  |  |  +--rw prefix?        srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-prefix
     |     |  |  |  +--rw prefix-list* [name] {srl_nokia-feat:acl-ip-prefix-list}?
     |     |  |  |  |  +--rw name    -> /acl/match-list/ipv6-prefix-list/name
     |     |  |  |  +--rw address?       srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  |  |  +--rw mask?          srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  |  +--rw dscp-set*         srl_nokia-comm:dscp {srl_nokia-feat:ip-acl-dscp-set}?
     |     |  |  +--rw icmp6
     |     |  |  |  +--rw type?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:icmp6-type
     |     |  |  |  +--rw code*   uint8
     |     |  |  +--rw next-header?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ip-protocol-type
     |     |  |  +--rw source-ip
     |     |  |     +--rw prefix?        srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-prefix
     |     |  |     +--rw prefix-list* [name] {srl_nokia-feat:acl-ip-prefix-list}?
     |     |  |     |  +--rw name    -> /acl/match-list/ipv6-prefix-list/name
     |     |  |     +--rw address?       srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  |     +--rw mask?          srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  +--rw transport
     |     |     +--rw destination-port
     |     |     |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |     |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |     |  +--rw range
     |     |     |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |     |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |     +--rw source-port
     |     |     |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |     |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |     |  +--rw range
     |     |     |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |     |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |     +--rw tcp-flags?          string
     |     +--rw action
     |     |  +--rw (action)?
     |     |  |  +--:(accept)
     |     |  |  |  +--rw accept!
     |     |  |  |     +--rw rate-limit
     |     |  |  |        +--rw system-cpu-policer?   -> /acl/policers/system-cpu-policer/name
     |     |  |  |        +--rw policer?              -> /acl/policers/policer/name {srl_nokia-feat:acl-policer}?
     |     |  |  +--:(drop)
     |     |  |  |  +--rw drop!
     |     |  |  +--:(copy)
     |     |  |     +--rw copy! {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     |     |  +--rw log?            boolean {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     |     +--ro statistics
     |     |  +--ro last-clear?           srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |     |  +--ro incomplete?           boolean {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     |     |  +--ro matched-packets?      srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |  +--ro last-match?           srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |     |  +--ro policer {srl_nokia-feat:acl-policer and not srl_nokia-feat:platform-vsrl}?
     |     |  |  +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |  |  +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |  |  +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |  |  +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |  +--ro system-cpu-policer
     |     |     +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |     +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |     +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |     +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     +--ro tcam-entries
     |        +--ro forwarding-complex* [complex-identifier]
     |           +--ro complex-identifier    string
     |           +--ro single-instance?      uint16
     |           +--ro input-total?          uint16 {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     |           +--ro output-total?         uint16 {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     +--rw interface* [interface-id]
     |  +--rw interface-id     string
     |  +--rw interface-ref
     |  |  +--rw interface?      -> /srl_nokia-if:interface/name
     |  |  +--rw subinterface?   -> /srl_nokia-if:interface[srl_nokia-if:name=current()/../interface]/subinterface/index
     |  +--rw input
     |  |  +--rw acl-filter* [name type]
     |  |  |  +--rw name     -> /acl/acl-filter/name
     |  |  |  +--rw type     -> /acl/acl-filter[name=current()/../name]/type
     |  |  |  +--ro entry* [sequence-id]
     |  |  |     +--ro sequence-id    -> /acl/acl-filter[name=current()/../../name][type=current()/../../type]/entry/sequence-id
     |  |  |     +--ro statistics {srl_nokia-feat:acl-subinterface-entry-statistics}?
     |  |  |     |  +--ro last-clear?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  |  |     |  +--ro incomplete?        boolean {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     |  |  |     |  +--ro matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |  |     |  +--ro last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  |  |     +--ro policer {srl_nokia-feat:subif-acl-policer}?
     |  |  |        +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |  |        +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |  |        +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |  |        +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |  +--ro statistics {srl_nokia-feat:subif-acl-policer}?
     |  |     +--ro last-clear?   srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  |     +--ro policer {srl_nokia-feat:subif-acl-policer}?
     |  |        +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |        +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |        +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |        +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  +--rw output {not srl_nokia-feat:platform-7215-a1}?
     |     +--rw acl-filter* [name type]
     |     |  +--rw name     -> /acl/acl-filter/name
     |     |  +--rw type     -> /acl/acl-filter[name=current()/../name]/type
     |     |  +--ro entry* [sequence-id]
     |     |     +--ro sequence-id    -> /acl/acl-filter[name=current()/../../name][type=current()/../../type]/entry/sequence-id
     |     |     +--ro statistics {srl_nokia-feat:acl-subinterface-entry-statistics}?
     |     |     |  +--ro last-clear?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |     |     |  +--ro incomplete?        boolean {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     |     |     |  +--ro matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |     |  +--ro last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |     |     +--ro policer {srl_nokia-feat:subif-acl-policer}?
     |     |        +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |        +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |        +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     |        +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |     +--ro statistics {srl_nokia-feat:subif-acl-policer}?
     |        +--ro last-clear?   srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro policer {srl_nokia-feat:subif-acl-policer}?
     |           +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |           +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |           +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |           +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     +--rw policers
     |  +--rw system-cpu-policer* [name]
     |  |  +--rw name                srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  |  +--rw entry-specific?     boolean
     |  |  +--rw peak-packet-rate?   uint32
     |  |  +--rw max-packet-burst?   uint32
     |  |  +--ro statistics
     |  |     +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |     +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |     +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |     +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |     +--ro last-clear?           srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  +--rw policer* [name] {srl_nokia-feat:acl-policer}?
     |     +--rw name              srl_nokia-comm:name
     |     +--rw entry-specific?   boolean {not srl_nokia-feat:fpcx}?
     |     +--rw scope?            enumeration {srl_nokia-feat:subif-acl-policer}?
     |     +--rw peak-rate?        uint32
     |     +--rw max-burst?        uint32
     |     +--ro statistics
     |        +--ro aggregate
     |           +--ro last-clear?           srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |           +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |           +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |           +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |           +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     +--ro datapath-programming
     |  +--ro forwarding-complex* [slot-id complex-id]
     |     +--ro slot-id                     uint8
     |     +--ro complex-id                  uint8
     |     +--ro programming-complete?       boolean
     |     +--ro last-completed-timestamp?   srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     +--rw match-list {srl_nokia-feat:acl-ip-prefix-list}?
     |  +--rw ipv4-prefix-list* [name]
     |  |  +--rw name           string
     |  |  +--rw description?   srl_nokia-comm:description
     |  |  +--rw prefix* [ipv4-prefix]
     |  |     +--rw ipv4-prefix    srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |  +--rw ipv6-prefix-list* [name]
     |     +--rw name           string
     |     +--rw description?   srl_nokia-comm:description
     |     +--rw prefix* [ipv6-prefix]
     |        +--rw ipv6-prefix    srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-prefix
     +--rw egress-mac-filtering?   boolean {srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-d2 or srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-d3 or srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-d4 or srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-d5}?

module: srl_nokia-bfd
  +--rw bfd! {srl_nokia-feat:bfd}?
     +--rw subinterface* [id]
     |  +--rw id                                   srl_nokia-comm:subinterface-no-mgmt
     |  +--rw admin-state?                         srl_nokia-comm:admin-state
     |  +--rw desired-minimum-transmit-interval?   uint32
     |  +--rw required-minimum-receive?            uint32
     |  +--rw detection-multiplier?                uint8
     |  +--rw minimum-echo-receive-interval?       uint32
     |  +--rw max-hop-count?                       uint8
     +--ro network-instance* [name]
     |  +--ro name    string
     |  +--ro peer* [local-discriminator]
     |     +--ro local-discriminator                 uint32
     |     +--ro oper-state?                         srl_nokia-comm:oper-state
     |     +--ro ipv6-link-local-interface?          string
     |     +--ro ipv4-unnumbered-interface?          string
     |     +--ro local-address?                      srl_nokia-comm:ip-address
     |     +--ro remote-address?                     srl_nokia-comm:ip-address
     |     +--ro remote-discriminator?               uint32
     |     +--ro subscribed-protocols?               string
     |     +--ro session-state?                      bfd-session-state
     |     +--ro remote-session-state?               bfd-session-state
     |     +--ro last-state-transition?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |     +--ro last-failure-time?                  srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |     +--ro failure-transitions?                uint64
     |     +--ro local-diagnostic-code?              bfd-diagnostic-code
     |     +--ro remote-diagnostic-code?             bfd-diagnostic-code
     |     +--ro remote-minimum-receive-interval?    uint32
     |     +--ro remote-control-plane-independent?   boolean
     |     +--ro active-transmit-interval?           uint32
     |     +--ro active-receive-interval?            uint32
     |     +--ro remote-multiplier?                  uint8
     |     +--ro te-policy-name?                     string
     |     +--ro te-policy-type?                     srl_nokia-te-policies:te-policy-type
     |     +--ro te-policy-segment-list-index?       uint32
     |     +--ro te-policy-protocol-origin?          te-policy-origin
     |     +--ro te-policy-segment-list-lsp-index?   uint32
     |     +--ro sr-policy-endpoint?                 srl_nokia-comm:ip-address
     |     +--ro async!
     |        +--ro last-packet-transmitted?    srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro last-packet-received?       srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro transmitted-packets?        srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        +--ro received-packets?           srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        +--ro up-transitions?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        +--ro received-errored-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        +--ro last-clear?                 srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     +--ro total-bfd-sessions?                       srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter32
     +--ro total-unmatched-bfd-packets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:micro-bfd-sessions {srl_nokia-feat:lag}?
        +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:lag-interface* [name]
           +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:name                                 -> /srl_nokia-if:interface/name
           +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:admin-state?                         srl_nokia-comm:admin-state
           +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:local-address?                       srl_nokia-comm:ip-address
           +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-address?                      srl_nokia-comm:ip-address
           +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:desired-minimum-transmit-interval?   uint32
           +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:required-minimum-receive?            uint32
           +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:detection-multiplier?                uint8
           +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:member-interface* [name]
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:name                                string
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:session-state?                      bfd-session-state
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-session-state?               bfd-session-state
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:last-state-transition?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:last-failure-time?                  srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:failure-transitions?                uint64
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:local-discriminator?                uint32
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-discriminator?               uint32
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:local-diagnostic-code?              bfd-diagnostic-code
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-diagnostic-code?             bfd-diagnostic-code
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-minimum-receive-interval?    uint32
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-control-plane-independent?   boolean
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:active-transmit-interval?           uint32
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:active-receive-interval?            uint32
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-multiplier?                  uint8
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:async!
                 +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:last-packet-transmitted?    srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
                 +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:last-packet-received?       srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
                 +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:transmitted-packets?        srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
                 +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:received-packets?           srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
                 +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:up-transitions?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
                 +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:received-errored-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
                 +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:last-clear?                 srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta

module: srl_nokia-interfaces
  +--rw interface* [name]
     +--rw name                              srl_nokia-comm:interface-all
     +--rw description?                      srl_nokia-comm:description
     +--rw admin-state?                      srl_nokia-comm:admin-state
     +--rw mtu?                              uint16
     +--rw loopback-mode?                    loopback-mode-type {not srl_nokia-feat:platform-vsrl}?
     +--ro ifindex?                          uint32
     +--ro oper-state?                       enumeration
     +--ro oper-down-reason?                 port-oper-down-reason
     +--ro last-change?                      srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     +--ro linecard?                         -> /srl_nokia-plat:platform/srl_nokia-lc:linecard/slot
     +--ro forwarding-complex?               -> /srl_nokia-plat:platform/srl_nokia-lc:linecard/forwarding-complex/name
     +--ro phy-group-members*                string {srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-d2 or srl_nokia-feat:platform-7730-sxr-1d-32d or srl_nokia-feat:platform-7250-ixr-x1b}?
     +--ro physical-channel*                 -> /interface/transceiver/channel/index
     +--ro forwarding-mode?                  enumeration {srl_nokia-feat:system-forwarding-mode}?
     +--ro statistics
     |  +--ro in-packets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  +--ro in-octets?               srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  +--ro in-unicast-packets?      srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  +--ro in-broadcast-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  +--ro in-multicast-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  +--ro in-discarded-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  +--ro in-error-packets?        srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  +--ro in-fcs-error-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  +--ro out-packets?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64

module: srl_nokia-network-instance
  +--rw network-instance* [name]
     +--rw name                                           srl_nokia-comm:restricted-name
     +--rw type?                                          identityref
     +--rw admin-state?                                   srl_nokia-comm:admin-state
     +--ro oper-state?                                    srl_nokia-comm:oper-state
     +--ro oper-down-reason?                              enumeration

     +--rw description?                                   srl_nokia-comm:description
     +--rw router-id?                                     srl_nokia-comm:dotted-quad
     +--rw mpls-forwarding
     |  +--rw forward-received-packets?   boolean
     +--rw ip-forwarding!

     |  +--rw receive-ipv6-check?   boolean
     |  +--rw last-resort-lookup
     |     +--rw network-instance?   -> /network-instance/name
     +--rw ip-load-balancing {srl-feat:ixr-dnx or srl-feat:trident3 or srl-feat:trident4 or srl-feat:fpcx}?
     |  +--rw resilient-hash-prefix* [ip-prefix]
     |     +--rw ip-prefix                srl_nokia-comm:ip-prefix
     |     +--rw hash-buckets-per-path?   uint8
     |     +--rw max-paths?               uint8
     +--rw inter-instance-policies {srl-feat:route-leaking}?
     |  +--rw apply-policy
     |     +--rw import-policy?   -> /srl-rpol:routing-policy/policy/name
     |     +--rw export-policy?   -> /srl-rpol:routing-policy/policy/name
     +--rw interface* [name]
     |  +--rw name                srl_nokia-netinst:network-instance-subintf-name
     |  +--rw interface-ref {srl-feat:interface-references}?
     |  |  +--rw interface?      -> /srl_nokia-if:interface/name
     |  |  +--rw subinterface?   -> /srl_nokia-if:interface[srl_nokia-if:name=current()/../interface]/subinterface/index
     |  +--ro oper-state?         srl_nokia-comm:oper-state
     |  +--ro oper-down-reason?   enumeration
     |  +--ro index?              uint64
     |  +--rw bridge-table! {srl-feat:bridged}?
     |     +--rw split-horizon-group?                 -> ../../../bridge-table/split-horizon-group/name {srl-feat:bridged and srl-feat:bt-split-horizon-groups}?

     |     +--ro multicast-forwarding?                srl_nokia-comm:multicast-type
     |     +--ro oper-mac-learning?                   srl_nokia-comm:oper-state

  +--rw tunnel {srl-feat:vxlan or srl-feat:pseudowire}?
     +--rw srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:vxlan-tunnel {srl_nokia-feat:vxlan}?
        +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:vtep* [address]
        |  +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:address        srl_nokia-comm:ip-address
        |  +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:index?         uint64
        |  +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:last-change?   srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
        |  +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:statistics {srl_nokia-feat:vxlan-stats}?
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-octets?               srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-packets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-discarded-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-octets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-packets?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-discarded-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
        |     +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:last-clear?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
        +--rw srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:statistics {srl_nokia-feat:vxlan-stats}?
           +--rw srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:admin-state?            srl_nokia-comm:admin-state
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-octets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-packets?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-discarded-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-octets?             srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:out-packets?            srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:last-clear?             srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
